Flag Changed on Mount Emba Aradom; Italian Forces Have a Good Chance of Winning the Invasion of Abyssinia; Loss of Fortress Causes Morale of Abyssinian Army to Plunge; Italian Forces Attack Abyssinian Left Wing from Two Directions 31

Rome: The Italian flag was planted on the summit of Mount Emba Aradom on the eve of the fortieth anniversary of the Italian defeat at Adwa. This flag, recently transported from Italy, was planted on the high peak by the father of a military officer who died in 1896. While the First Blackshirt Legion occupied Emba Aradom, the Italian Sarda Division captured Faraga to the east, and the Alpine Division reached Tuggura to the west. Thus, the entire twenty-mile-long mountain ridge is in Italian hands, which is the most dangerous place to attack Abyssinia from the north. The Italian army climbed the mountain and occupied the area without any resistance. It was initially expected that the Italian left wing would begin its advance only after the Danakil and Takkaze zones were cleared. However, because the Abyssinian Emperor's new army came to the rescue from the north, the Italian General Staff decided to attack quickly and achieved this victory. Italian aircraft are now bombing the villages and towns where the Abyssinian Emperor is stationed. The morale of the Abyssinian army is said to have plunged after seeing the remnants of Abyssinian General Mulugo's forces fleeing south. It is generally believed that the Italian victory has determined the future of the war in favor of Italy. The occupation of Emba Aradom has three important implications: Historically, Italy's previous humiliation has been avenged; Politically, the gateway to the south has been opened, and the morale of Abyssinian soldiers and their loyalty to the Abyssinian Emperor will be greatly affected; Militarily, this strategic location is easy to defend and can control all roads from the south to the Tigray and Danakil zones. The Italian army has now begun operations to encircle the troops of Abyssinian Generals Seyoum and Kassa in the Danakil zone. The Italian army has set out from Aksum and other places to outflank the Abyssinian left wing. According to a report from General Badoglio, commander of the Italian forces in East Africa, the battle has been ongoing since dawn on February 28th. Two divisions of the Italian army are attacking Abyssinian General Kassa's army from the north and south. (29th Reuters Dispatch)

Italian Forces Advance While Pursuing Victory; Southern Route to Launch Soon 32

Rome: General Badoglio, High Commissioner of Italian East Africa and Commander-in-Chief of the Expeditionary Forces, recently issued Public Notice No. 140, stating, "The Italian army on the Eritrean front in the north launched an attack on the troops of Abyssinian General Kassa's forward command from both the north and south at dawn yesterday, February 28. The battle is still ongoing." (29th Havas Dispatch)

Rome: The Ministry of the Army issued a war report today stating that according to a telegram from General Badoglio, Commander of the Italian Forces in Africa, the Italian First Army Corps has now occupied Emba Aradom. This decisive victory is sufficient to erase the humiliation of General Toselli's defeat in 1896. According to reports, Toselli was the captain of the Fourth Regiment of Eritrea and was defeated by the Abyssinian army at Mount Emba Aradom in 1896, retreating to Adwa, where he eventually died in battle. The Italians were overjoyed upon hearing this victory report today. (28th National News Agency Dispatch)

The Italian army on the northern route occupied Mount Emba Aradom yesterday after fighting a fierce battle with the Abyssinian army for twenty-four hours. This mountain is actually 3,438 meters high and controls all the main roads in central Abyssinia. It is indeed a fortress on the northern route. Now that it has been occupied by the Italian army, it can be used to set up a new position. Even if the Abyssinian army wants to counterattack, it may not be able to do so. (28th Havas Dispatch)

League of Nations to Meet Tomorrow; Oil Embargo to Be Delayed; Impossible to Implement at This Time? Armed Conflict Creates Self-Destruction 33

London: The League of Nations' eighteen-nation small committee is scheduled to meet in Geneva on March 2nd to discuss the oil embargo issue. Foreign Minister Eden will go to Geneva on Sunday, March 1st, to attend the meeting. According to general predictions, the committee's discussions will likely result in the creation of another technical committee to study the issue of embargoing other raw materials due to the impossibility of implementing the oil embargo at this time. Previously, the small committee had organized a technical committee to study the oil embargo, and its conclusion was that the embargo would be difficult to implement without the participation of the United States. This conclusion will likely be put on record by the small committee, and the implementation date will be decided when the time is right. However, the embargo on other raw materials (i.e., iron, steel, and coal) was already decided in principle in the resolution passed by the eighteen-nation small committee on November 5th of last year. The implementation will also follow the example of organizing a technical committee to study it. If this procedure is adopted, the activities of the participating sanctioning countries will not be suspended, and the tense situation between those countries and Italy will not be aggravated due to the delayed implementation of the stricter sanctions. This is what the British delegation to the Naval Conference hopes for, as Britain hopes that this delaying tactic will soften Italy's attitude and prevent it from refusing to sign the pact. Diplomatic sources also say that the talk of Italy and Germany working together is rampant. Although this is a tactic and may not be realized, delaying the implementation of stricter sanctions is also enough to prevent Italy and Germany from getting closer. (28th Havas Dispatch)

Hitler Proposes Closer Relations with France; Otherwise, Serious Consequences Will Ensue 34

London: Two newspapers in Paris and London have published talks of German leader Hitler. In this talk, Hitler directly proposed closer relations with France and warned France that serious consequences would ensue if it ignored this gesture. France is paying close attention to this talk. According to a Reuters dispatch from Paris, French newspapers are likely to view this proposal with skepticism and doubt the conditions for a genuine approach proposed by Hitler. It is said that France is willing to proceed with the German leader's proposal under the following conditions: Germany rejoins the League of Nations; Germany limits its armaments; and the status quo in Central Europe is fully respected. A Reuters dispatch from Berlin stated that despite the Franco-Soviet mutual assistance pact, Germany still hopes to seek a lasting understanding with France. (19th Reuters Dispatch)

Berlin: The "Deutsche Volksbeobachter," the mouthpiece of Minister of Economics Schacht, recently published a commentary to explain the views of German economic leaders on the diplomatic situation. Between the lines, it hinted at skepticism about the possible results of the Nazi Party's foreign policy and suggested, in polite terms, that the authorities change their foreign policy. It stated, "After Germany's rearmament, its prestige has been restored, but it is essential to understand the extent to which this restored prestige has been destroyed by our country's foreign policy. Germany is currently surrounded, which can be seen in three important reasons: First, the Franco-Soviet mutual assistance treaty; second, the rapprochement between Britain and Russia and the cooling of relations between Britain and Germany; and third, the policies implemented by the Little Entente countries in Central Europe and the Balkans. Regarding the Franco-Soviet mutual assistance treaty, the Locarno Pact is bound to be revised. Germany can express its good intentions and offer new guarantees to other countries as an exchange condition, and it can renegotiate the Sky Pact with Britain and France, provided that Germany's equal rights are recognized and the Italian-Abyssinian dispute can be effectively resolved. If Italy wins, its economy and finances will need assistance from other countries and will naturally move closer to Britain, which, having no danger to fear after the end of the East African War, will also be happy to do so. As for the relationship between Britain and Russia, Britain's imperialist policy hopes that Russia will not interfere and is willing to maintain peace in Europe in order to confront Japan. The newspaper also denied the claims that Japan and Germany have already concluded a political or military agreement, saying that if Britain gives Germany some benefits in the allocation of raw materials, Germany will certainly be optimistic about certain plans of Britain. Britain will eventually see this. In addition, since the economies of Germany and Russia are interdependent, their relations can return to normal, so that no incident will occur in Europe, which is also in Britain's interest. As for Czech Prime Minister Hodza, although he has made great efforts in the Balkans, it is difficult to form a group from the Czech Republic to the Black Sea to assist in the policy of other countries surrounding Germany, but Germany must be vigilant." (29th Havas Dispatch)

Moscow: All newspapers carried editorials welcoming the French Chamber of Deputies' ratification of the Franco-Soviet pact. Izvestia stated that German newspapers were needlessly alarming and falsely claiming that someone was surrounding Germany. This move was only intended to pre-arrange proof that Germany's current and strengthened aggressive policies were legitimate. The sooner the French Senate ratifies this pact, the more clearly it will show that Germany's intimidation tactics are a waste of effort. If Germany can understand this point, then it can reason with others and have the opportunity to join the collective peace system on its own initiative. The Soviet government, like France, is willing to live peacefully with Germany, and not only does it not want to refuse to accept Germany's reasonable demands for peace, but it even promotes them. The French Chamber of Deputies' decision to reject Germany's threats is a positive factor in consolidating European peace. At a time when far-eastern military fascists are trying to break through all resistance and launch a war, the significance of this pact being ratified is even more important. The consolidation of European peace is also a positive factor in consolidating peace in the Far East. All efforts by Europe, America, and Japan to maintain peace in Eurasia must cooperate most closely, regardless of the actions of military adventurers. The Soviet Union will continue to resolutely pursue its policy of peace and gather all its strength to maintain peace with a calm attitude. However, this policy is by no means aimed at any country. Pravda stated that the French Chamber of Deputies passed the ratification of the Franco-Soviet pact to consolidate peace and strengthen cooperation with the Soviet Union, as the Soviet Union is a strong pillar of peace among all countries. The reactionary right wing in France tried to isolate France. They spoke as aggressive forces and German fascist spies to sabotage the pact, but the Chamber of Deputies has already rejected them. In light of the current world situation, there are extremely disturbing events in various countries. During this period, the united efforts of all anti-fascist forces and all anti-war countries have special significance in terms of human destiny. The Franco-Soviet pact is an example of a solution to consolidate collective security and peace. (28th TASS Dispatch)

Britain Plans to Dig a Canal in Scotland to Connect East and West Coast Naval Ports; Also, Add Two New Naval Ports on the West Coast to Allow Warships to Reach Between the North Sea and the Atlantic 35

London: According to a special report from our agency's reporter, British naval experts are now planning to connect the main naval bases on the east and west coasts into one by digging a canal between the Firth of Clyde and the Firth of Forth, so as to connect the city of Edinburgh on the Firth of Forth with the city of Glasgow on the Firth of Clyde, and the largest battleships can be transferred from the North Sea to the Atlantic or from the Atlantic to the North Sea without having to go through the open sea. In addition, it is planned to open two main naval bases on the west coast, one in Milford Haven, Wales, which will be 20 kilometers long, and one in the Firth of Forth. Financial circles believe that the Admiralty has already purchased large tracts of land in Milford Haven. (29th Havas)

Anglo-American-French Naval Agreement: Signing Expected Next Week 37

London: Since Italy expressed its unwillingness to sign the naval agreement, Britain has suggested that Britain, France, and the United States sign an agreement, supplemented by a separate agreement between Britain and Germany. The representatives of France and the United States have already requested instructions from their respective governments. This tripartite agreement is expected to be signed within the next week. Although the French representative has not yet received instructions from his government, it is generally believed that France will not raise significant objections to the tripartite agreement, nor will it require China to inform France of Germany's shipbuilding program after the Anglo-German agreement is concluded, lest Britain reject it. Naval figures also stated that in any future agreement between Britain and Germany, Germany will insist that the terms not be communicated to other countries, and will use this as a condition for signing the agreement. (Havas News Agency dispatch of the 29th)

London: The future progress of the naval conference depends on the French delegation. The delegation is currently seeking instructions from Paris on whether to continue the tripartite negotiations. It is reported that France hopes to obtain an understanding that Italy will be willing to sign the naval treaty when the Italo-Ethiopian issue is resolved. Both Italy and France have no major concerns regarding the technical aspects of drafting the treaty, so it is expected that an understanding between France and Italy will facilitate the treaty's conclusion. (Reuters dispatch of the 29th)

London: After Italy refused to sign the naval agreement yesterday, Britain suggested that Britain, France, and the United States sign a naval treaty. The French representative has already requested instructions from his government. Once instructions from Paris arrive, Britain and France can continue their talks. Naval conference personnel generally believe that France may accept the signing of a tripartite treaty, but on the condition that it receives some satisfaction on the issue of battleships. Satisfaction could mean reducing the 35,000-ton figure, or, even if not reducing it, shortening its validity period. In addition, France also intends to propose a method to be included in the naval treaty so that Italy can sign and join it when it deems appropriate. Regarding the issue of Britain and Germany signing a naval treaty, the German Ambassador to Britain, Herr von Hoesch, has requested instructions from his government on what is appropriate. Once instructions from Berlin arrive, Britain and Germany will also continue their talks. According to naval figures, Germany will definitely accept signing, but beforehand will request to know the final terms of the treaty from Britain. Furthermore, Germany also wants to know whether the Soviet Union will also sign and participate, and what intentions it holds. Regarding the issue of the Soviet Union signing and participating, it is now known that Britain and the Soviet Union have held talks, but only to exchange information, and no further discussions have been made. (The Soviet representative is Colonel Tkachenko, Naval Attaché at the Soviet Embassy in Britain.) (Havas News Agency dispatch of the 28th)

Paris: According to information obtained by this agency's diplomatic correspondent, Italy has already stated its refusal to sign the future naval treaty. Therefore, France believes that unless guarantee clauses are added to the treaty to reserve leeway for the French Navy, France cannot accept signing it. Regarding this matter, the French delegation to the naval conference has requested instructions from the government. This afternoon, Deputy Director of Political Affairs of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Massigli, held talks with the Minister of the Navy, Pietri. It is now known that after these talks, these instructions will largely be sent to London tonight. It is reported that the instructions will order the delegation to negotiate with the Italian delegation to ensure that Italy issues a formal document stating that even if it does not sign the treaty, it will still promise to be bound by its terms. In the event that Italy rejects this request, then guarantee clauses should be added to the naval treaty to reserve leeway for the French Navy, and then France can accept signing it. However, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs here still believes that after the meeting of the League of Nations' Committee of Eighteen, Italy may change its decision regarding the signing issue. In addition, France has another objection regarding the method of signing a tripartite treaty, which is related to the conditions for Germany's participation in signing. What France requires is that Germany, based on the treaty drafted by Britain and Germany, should notify Britain of the shipbuilding program, and Britain should then notify France. It is expected that next week, when Foreign Minister Flandin meets with British Foreign Secretary Eden in Geneva, he will specifically mention this point. (Havas News Agency dispatch of the 28th)

London: According to information obtained by this agency's reporter, the Italian Chief Delegate to the naval conference, Ambassador Grandi, has informed Foreign Secretary Eden that Italy has no objection if Britain, France, and the United States sign a naval treaty. This morning, he also met with the American Chief Delegate, Davis, and stated that Italy cannot sign the naval treaty "under the current circumstances." He said that the technical objections raised by Italy are not irreparable, and that the reason for refusing to sign is actually due to the continued implementation of sanctions and the continued pressure of the British Navy on Italy in the Mediterranean. It is generally believed that after Grandi presented the above explanation, American sympathy for Italy's position has increased. Davis then met with Foreign Secretary Eden in the afternoon to discuss the situation regarding the signing of the naval treaty by the three countries. According to information obtained by this agency's reporter, Eden informed Davis of the position taken by Germany regarding the signing of the British naval treaty, saying that Germany is now waiting for France to provide a response before making a concrete decision. It is said that Germany has raised several technical objections, but their nature is not important and they are easy to resolve. In addition, the French representative, Rear Admiral Robert, met with Italian Rear Admiral Piglia, and Piglia explained Italy's position, stating that not only is formal signing rejected, but even initialing is not desired. It is heard that if the sanctions are not lifted for one day, even if the Committee of Eighteen does not decide to intensify sanctions, Italy's above attitude will not change for one day. (Havas News Agency dispatch of the 28th)

US Navy to Open Panama Canal: Spring Maneuvers to be Held on April 10 38

Washington: According to an announcement released by the Army Department today, the US fleet will sail to Panama on April 10 to conduct spring maneuvers and practice defensive tactics for the Panama Canal. (Guomin News Agency dispatch of the 28th)

Washington: A delegation representing shipyards on the Pacific coast today went to the House Naval Affairs Committee to request that the shipbuilding industry on both coasts be given a 6% advantage in the construction of 54 auxiliary vessels. They cited the situation of the US fleet in the Pacific and the Far East to prove the necessity of restoring the shipbuilding industry on the west coast. Mrs. Kahn, a member of the delegation, stated that "If we have eyes but do not pay attention to the situation in the Pacific, the harm is much greater than having no eyes. This is a matter of self-defense, and the Naval Affairs Committee cannot ignore it." Another representative, named Torrence, also said, "A single spark can start a prairie fire. A world war could break out at any moment. If a war breaks out, everyone knows where it will come from. Think about our position when a war breaks out in the Pacific. If the Panama Canal has any accident, how can ships on the west coast sail to the east coast for repairs?" (Reuters dispatch of the 28th) The current US Neutrality Act, since September of last year,

Washington: Since the Neutrality Act took effect last September, it was originally scheduled to expire tomorrow. Both the Senate and the House of Representatives recently passed a new bill to extend the validity of the current law until May 1 of next year. President Roosevelt is also scheduled to sign it tonight so that it will take effect from the first of next month. At that time, the President may issue a declaration stating that the US government still maintains neutrality regarding the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. (Havas News Agency dispatch of the 28th)

Washington: Secretary of State Hull yesterday delivered a radio address to the countries of North and South America, in which he said, "The United States has helped to stop the war between Bolivia and Paraguay, and President Roosevelt has also proposed convening a Pan-American Peace Conference. All of this is sufficient to prove that the United States is determined to maintain peace and tranquility on the American continent. Furthermore, the Good Neighbor Policy advocated by the United States is no longer just a hope, a goal, but has become a reality." Hull then recounted the policies implemented by the US government toward the countries of the Americas, with the following being particularly noteworthy: * The new treaty between the US and Cuba has abolished the Platt Amendment, which allowed the US to interfere in Cuba's internal affairs. * The withdrawal of US Marines stationed in Haiti. * The US is currently conducting negotiations with Panama to conclude a new treaty to replace the old treaty of 1903. * Commercial treaties have been concluded with five countries in the Americas based on reciprocity. (Havas News Agency dispatch of the 29th)

Coup in Chile Fails: Fifteen Retired Military Personnel Arrested 39

Santiago, Chile: Military personnel and civilians here also plotted a coup, but because the plot was not secret, it was defeated by the government's preemptive action. Officials received advance notice and immediately deployed an ambush, allowing the rebels to enter the Army Department and occupy the General Headquarters. However, General Novoa, the Army Commander-in-Chief whom the rebels wanted to capture, was not in the department. None of the rebels escaped, and a total of fifteen people were arrested. (Guomin News Agency dispatch of the 28th)

Capital of Chile: Captain Wossler, a retired officer, led a group of other retired officers yesterday afternoon in an attempt to stage a coup, intending to detain Chief of Staff General Novoa. The government immediately mobilized the National Defense Forces to suppress them and arrested fifteen people. At the same time, all government offices were ordered to strictly guard their doors, and soldiers were not allowed to leave their barracks. The regular army did not participate in the rebellion. President Alessandri happened to be at a seaside villa. Upon hearing the news, he rushed back to the capital and took drastic measures. Although the unrest has begun in various parts of the country, everything is currently peaceful and stable. According to official statements, the masterminds behind this rebellion are retired officers and several prominent politicians, namely, members of the party of former President Ibáñez. (Havas News Agency dispatch of the 28th)

US Tax Plan Totals $1.2 Billion 40

Washington: President Roosevelt today announced to reporters his tax plan of $1,137,000,000, as follows: * $120,000,000 to pay veterans' bonuses. * $1,017,000,000 to be used as agricultural program funding for 1936-1937. The method of raising funds for the agricultural program is to collect a fixed tax of $500,000,000 per year to compensate for the loss after the Supreme Court ruled the Agricultural Adjustment Act invalid. The decision is to collect a temporary tax for three years to make up for the agricultural adjustment tax lost by the Treasury Department. The remaining adjustment taxes will be supplemented by collecting special income taxes. (Guomin News Agency dispatch of the 28th)

Strong Winds Still Prevail in Tianjin: Ice Floes Carry Ships Out to Sea; Whereabouts of Customs Lightship "Haiming" and Four Other Vessels Unknown; Taku-Tanggu Intertidal Area Frozen Solid, Ships Unable to Navigate 47

Tianjin: A strong northwest wind rose on the night of the 28th. The Taku Bar lightship and nine vessels, including the stranded "Changcheng Maru" and "Chosho Maru," were blown out to sea. On the 29th, the "Tianxing" tried to force her way outside to investigate. The "Changcheng" and "Chosho" had already sailed to Dalian. The "Zhonghe," "Chang'an," and "Zengli" drifted ten nautical miles outside the port, fortunately without danger. The whereabouts of the "Haiming" and four other vessels are unknown, and various parties are searching for them. After the lightship drifted away, there were no navigation marks, and all vessels were afraid of danger when entering and leaving the port, so they stopped sailing. (Special dispatch of the 29th)

Tianjin: After days of tides, the brash ice inside and outside the Xiaodagu cannot be broken. Although the northwest wind is strong, it is of no help. The Tianjin shipping industry again dispatched Wang Gengsan as a representative to the Haihe Engineering Bureau on the 29th to negotiate the prompt concentration of icebreaking vessel force to break the ice first, so that the wind blows it out of the port and open the waterway. The Haihe Engineering Bureau's ice-cleaning, ice-diving, and ice-breaking vessels are all frozen solid near the Heigu and Dagu Forts. It is necessary to rent another vessel to break the ice. (Special dispatch of the 29th)

Tianjin: The ships trapped outside Dagu are now in greater danger, because the northwest wind is strong, and the ice floes are moved by the wind, carrying the ships out to sea. According to news obtained here tonight, the ships trapped in Dagu are no longer visible. It is believed that there are two Taikoo ships and two Japanese ships among them, as well as several Chinese merchant vessels. The customs vessel "Haining" has also drifted out to sea with the ice. People in the shipping industry are now very anxious. (Reuters dispatch of the 29th)

Tianjin: The missing vessels blown away by the wind are the Taku Bar lightship of the Tianjin Customs, and three other vessels belonging to the British Taikoo Company. No news has been received either. The Tianjin Shipping Company dispatched the "Tianxing" on the 1st to sail outside the port again to search. On the 29th, the "Tianxing" worked outside Dagu for eight hours. By the evening, it had rescued the Japanese vessel "Ruzan Maru" and the "Shunli" of the Zhengji Company, and had provided food and coal to other trapped vessels. As of the evening of the 29th, the wind direction outside Dagu was still northwest, but the ice was thick and solid. The ice mountains in the Tanggu-Dagu section were stacked on top of each other and could not be blown out of the port, so the ships trapped outside the port could have sailed in, but because the ice inside the port had not melted, they could not move forward. (Special dispatch of the 29th)

Key Points of the Two Principles of the National Assembly 49

Nanjing: After Sun Ke approved the drafting of the two principles of the National Assembly Organization Law and the Representative Election Law to Fu Bingchang and 23 others, Fu et al. scheduled a meeting for next week. It is heard that the key points of the National Assembly Organization Law include that all members of the Central Executive and Supervisory Committees may attend, and all alternate members of the Central Executive and Supervisory Committees, the Chairman of the National Government, and the heads of various Yuan, Ministries, and Commissions may attend as non-voting delegates. The powers of the National Assembly include formulating the Constitution and exercising the special powers conferred upon it by the Constitution. The key points of the Representative Election Law include the election method, occupational elections, and local elections, and the number of representatives is tentatively set at 800 to 1,200. Occupational elections account for 40%, and local elections account for 60%. The election of overseas Chinese representatives is handled by the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission. Separate regulations exist for elections in border areas and the military. (Central News Agency dispatch of the 29th)

As for the Debt Consolidation Fund, 5 million yuan has been allocated annually from customs duties since 1929. As of recently, excluding interest, it has reached 30 million yuan. League of Nations Committee on Technical Cooperation with China to Meet Tomorrow; Ambassador Guo to Attend 85

Geneva: The Committee on Technical Cooperation with China, established by the League of Nations Council, is scheduled to meet next Monday (i.e., March 2nd) to formulate the outline of the work for the year 1936. This committee was established in 1933, with the Chairman of the Council as the Chairman and composed of representatives from seven countries: China, the United Kingdom, Denmark, Spain, France, Italy, and Romania. There is also an American observer attending the meeting. The committee's task is to handle the cooperation issues between the various technical agencies affiliated with the League of Nations and the National Economic Council of China. Whenever the Chinese government has a request regarding cooperation issues, it provides opinions to the League of Nations Council for adoption and implementation. There are currently five League of Nations experts serving in China: one specializing in rural cooperation, one specializing in silk improvement, two transportation experts, and one medical expert. (28th Havas dispatch)

Geneva: Guo Taiqi arrived here on the morning of the 29th and will attend the League of Nations Committee on Technical Cooperation with China on March 2nd. He will return to London on the night of the 2nd to host a reception for the Chinese Antiquities Exhibition on the 3rd. (29th Central News Agency dispatch)

Professor of the University of Paris Discusses China's Current Situation Again; Construction in Various Aspects is Actively Underway 86

Paris: Professor Aiscara of the Faculty of Law and the Chinese College of the University of Paris, who once served as a legal advisor to the Chinese government and is well-versed in Chinese affairs, recently made a statement to our reporter, saying that China has its inherent virtues, passed down through generations and becoming a model. However, adhering to outdated rules has led to stagnation, while its neighboring nations have been very active. Under their pressure, China has had to make concessions, resulting in unequal treaties that the majority of the Chinese people cannot tolerate. Therefore, the main problem in China today is to revise traditional ideas to suit the current trend. Construction in various aspects within China is now actively underway. Although there are many aspects, they are closely connected. In terms of economic construction, the Chinese people have gradually realized the importance of this endeavor. Therefore, all efforts are being steadily implemented. I have stayed in China for four years and have witnessed various improvements. There are now many model cities, such as Hangzhou, Guangzhou, Beiping, and Shanghai. The streets are clean and tidy, without a single piece of paper. In rural areas, where new-style medicine was previously unknown, health movements are now being actively carried out, and model villages are springing up everywhere. The civil servants in various institutions are young and energetic and are able to be loyal to their duties and serve the public interest. The progress in transportation is particularly noteworthy. For example, within Shandong Province, 6,500 kilometers of highways have been built in two years, with 800 buses operating regularly. The domestic aviation industry has also made rapid progress, which is very efficient in business. In terms of education, schools are springing up in remote areas, and all children know that cleanliness and orderliness can demonstrate patriotism. All of this is true and not an exaggeration. In addition, China's political construction and economic revival are proceeding hand in hand, with the aim of building a strong central government in accordance with the principles advocated by Mr. Sun Yat-sen. Furthermore, China has always valued culture and morality, and a new movement has now emerged in this area, namely the "New Life Movement," which aims to prevent traditional ideas from being lost and to adapt them to the needs of the new era. It has spread widely and has achieved great results. (28th Havas dispatch)

Orders 90

The State Reserve Order of the 29th stipulates that the Military Service Law will be implemented from March 1, 25th year [of the Republic of China]. This is ordered. Also ordered: The Provisional Regulations for Adding the Title of Lieutenant General of the Army, which have now been formulated, are hereby promulgated. This is ordered. Provisional Regulations for Adding the Title of Lieutenant General of the Army: Article 1: If a Lieutenant General of the Army meets the regulations for promotion to General according to Article 5, Paragraph 5 of the Provisional Regulations for Appointment of Army Officers, due to limitations in the number of personnel, he may first be given the title of General. Article 2: When there is a vacancy for a Second-Class General of the Army, it shall be specially filled by a Lieutenant General who has already been given the title of General. Article 3: The number of Lieutenant Generals of the Army who have been given the title of General shall be limited to the number of Generals of the Army. Article 4: A Lieutenant General who has been given the title of General shall have the same uniform and regulations as a Second-Class General of the Army, but his salary shall still be paid according to the highest salary level of a Lieutenant General. Article 5: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. Also ordered: The amendment to Article 11 of the Provisional Regulations on the Transfer of Prisoners to Cultivate Land is hereby promulgated. This is ordered. Also ordered: Chen Wenlin is hereby appointed as the Director of the Naval Aviation Department. This is ordered.

Special Education Broadcasting Publication

Geography Lecture: Why We Should Study Foreign Geography (3) 91

— Huang Guozhang, Professor of the Department of Geography, Central University

From what has been said above, we can know that Japan's relations with China have their own special geographical background. If we want to have a considerable understanding of Japan's international relations, we must first have a considerable understanding of Japanese geography. This is only in terms of Japan. The situation of other countries is mostly the same. Although the international situation is ever-changing, its roots are all geographical factors. The United Kingdom helped Abyssinia to resist Italy, on the one hand, to protect the route to the Far East, and on the other hand, to protect the water source of the upper Nile so as not to affect the agriculture along the lower Nile within the territory, while Italy, which is established on the peninsula, is either a mountainous area or a barren land except for the northern sandy river basin. Mineral resources are scarce, and the production of raw materials is extremely rare. A large part of them depends on foreign imports, so the war of aggression against A attracted the economic severance of 38 members of the League of Nations. Although the implementation of this economic sanction has been less than two months, the pain felt in Italy has been very deep. The soaring prices of everything have become a very common phenomenon. Daily necessities are strictly tightened. The original three meals a day are now changed to two meals. Government agencies have shortened office hours, stores have also shortened business hours, and elevators in each household have mostly been abandoned. Electric trains will also reduce the number of trains in order to save electricity; public buses will also be temporarily suspended to save petroleum, and the government extremely encourages walking, and other situations can be imagined. This further proves the close relationship between the countries now. It is agreed that the world has become a whole unit in terms of economy. No country can exist alone, and the importance of foreign geographical knowledge is self-evident.

The second reason for studying foreign geography is to understand China's position in the international community. A country's international status has a deep relationship with the three elements of establishing a country, namely, land, people, and the common national concept of the people. The so-called land includes land ownership, the size of the land area, the productivity of the land, the underground wealth, natural protection, internal natural communication, external natural connection, and the position of the land on the ground, etc. These are all questions that must be considered in geography: The so-called people include the number of people, the size of the people's ability to use nature (the degree of education and the progress of economic construction, etc.), the size of the people's purchasing power (the size of the market and the cost of wages, etc.), the nature of the people (obedience, fear, fortitude, decisiveness, etc.), and the ethnicity to which the people belong, etc. These are also all questions that must be addressed in geography; As for the common national concept of the people, it is a product of the interrelationship between the people and the land, because no matter which country's people, most of the daily necessities they need are due to their use of the land of their own country. They have the deepest knowledge and the most concern for the land of their own country. Only from this deep understanding and concern can a common national concept be aroused.

A good government can promote the interrelationship between the people and the land of the whole country. Personal power is limited, and it is impossible to deal with nature alone in everything. For example, the improvement of water conservancy, the improvement of transportation, the improvement and selection of seeds and livestock, the promotion of products, and many other similar problems all depend on the cooperation of the majority of the people. And there must also be a good government to make overall plans for the people, supervise and promote them, and do their best to protect them, so that the land can be used to its fullest extent and people can be used to their fullest extent. Moreover, the needs of the people's lives will never be fully supplied by the local area. In addition to a part of the supply from abroad, most of it is taken from other parts of the country. From the perspective of economic organization, a country is actually a whole economic unit. If we rely solely on the strength of the people and there is no good government to use the strength of the people to deal with all aspects of nature, how can we enable the people of the whole country to make appropriate use of the land of the whole country and collect mutually beneficial effects? How can it make the people of the whole country feel a sense of interdependence and inseparability from every part of the country, thereby cultivating a common national concept, so all the facilities of a good government, whether internal or external, should be aimed at increasing the ability of the people to use the land, thereby improving the living conditions of the people, so I can say that the common national concept arises from the interrelationship between the people and the land, and a good government is sufficient to promote the interrelationship between the people and the land.

The ancients said: "Know yourself and your enemy, and you will win every battle." Establishing a country under the current complex international situation, it is agreed that there must be clarity in knowing yourself and your enemy. Those who hold political power must understand the international status of the country's land and people, and the degree of development of the common national concept of the people, and the general people should also have a considerable understanding of this. The geography of one's own country focuses on knowing oneself, and the geography of foreign countries focuses on knowing the other, but in addition to knowing the other, one understands oneself even more deeply. The international status of one's own country can only be reflected after understanding foreign geography, and the country's foreign policy has a certain goal. Now, compare the United States and China to see the importance of the two countries in the international community.

There are many similarities between China and the United States, the most important of which are eight: The two countries are located at the same latitude. The coastlines of both countries are very long, and they both have good harbors and easy access to various places. Both countries have large river basins suitable for agriculture and are the world's main agricultural countries. Both countries are countries that can be self-sufficient in food. Both countries are agricultural export countries. Both countries have abundant mineral resources, which are sufficient for the development of heavy industry. Both countries are rich in manpower. Both countries are rich in natural water power.

As for the differences between the two countries, they can be explained in two aspects: (A) Aspects in which China exceeds the United States: China's area is larger than that of the United States by a ratio of 4:3 to 3.7. China's population is more than three times that of the United States, with a ratio of 45 to 1. The number of Chinese farmers is eight to nine times that of the United States. China's main agricultural products have a larger output than the United States, including rice, soybeans, sorghum, and millet. China's mineral products that are more abundant than those of the United States include antimony, tungsten, and tin. China's natural defense situation is more favorable than that of the United States, with high mountains, deserts, and plateaus in the northwest, and a coastline in the southeast with layers of protection. (B) Aspects in which the United States exceeds China: The area of ​​cultivated land in the heavenly kingdom is one-half times larger than that of China. The average area of ​​cultivated land obtained by each farmer in the United States is 40 times larger than that in China. The main agricultural crops in the United States that are more abundant than those in China include wheat, cotton, tobacco, and corn. The mineral products in the United States, such as coal, are 20 times more abundant than those in China, pig iron is 50 times more abundant than those in China, and the difference between oil and copper mines is even greater. The number of factory workers in the United States is ten times that of China. The number of railway miles in the United States is more than 20 times that of China. The number of automobile miles in the United States is 50 times that of China. The number of sea vessel tonnage in the United States is five times that of China. The number of spindles in the United States is nine times that of China. The number of textile machines in the United States is 21 times that of China. The value of foreign export trade in the United States is nine times that of China; the value of import trade is five times that of China. The average value of foreign trade per person in the United States is 20 times that of China.

From such a simple comparison, we can see the importance of the position of China and the United States in the international community. At the same time, we can also see that the various conditions in the natural environment of China and the United States are not far apart, and are generally very similar. The biggest difference between the two countries is almost entirely in the human aspect. In other words: China's land is favorable, but the Chinese people are not as capable as the Americans in using its benefits, which has led to a huge difference in the position of China and the United States in the international community. What about the comparison of the international status of China and Britain, China and France, China and Germany, China and Japan, China and Russia, and China and other countries in the world? Of course, it can only be seen by studying foreign geography.

This kind of comparison not only reveals the weaknesses of our country, but also shows the advantages of our country. For example, the large population of our country is the crown of the world, and we can use this advantage to improve our country's position in the international community. As long as we use scientific new inventions to develop the rich resources of our country and develop various industries, so that the 450 million people in the country can produce an average of one more yuan of goods per year, we can increase the value of human living materials in the world by 450 million yuan; at the same time, if each person can buy an average of one yuan more goods per year, it can increase the purchasing power of the world by 450 million yuan; in other words, it is equal to increasing the total value of trade in the world by several hundred million yuan. If this number is distributed to the world's 2 billion people, each person can get an average of 45 cents. The higher our productivity and purchasing power, the greater the impact on the international market. In addition, our country also has many unique mineral products such as antimony and tungsten mines; there are also many agricultural products that occupy a very superior position in the world market, such as tung oil, soybeans, raw silk, cotton, tea, peanuts, etc.; as long as we can use cheap labor to increase the output of goods and improve the quality of goods, our country's position on the international stage can definitely be improved. (To be continued)

Glimpses of Life in the Desert (14) 92

— Jin Dui

17. Historical Sites in the Suburbs of Xijing

(A) Within the City: (Centered on the Shovel Tower) East: East is East Main Street (i.e., Zhongshan Road). South of the road is Kaiyuan Temple. Going further east for half the distance, turn left and north to find Revolution Park. Returning to East Main Street and going east to the city wall is the East Mountain Temple, which has ancient murals. Then turn west and halfway down the street, turn left and walk south through Duanju Gate. Pass through the eastern entrance of East Wood Market to East Hall Gate, then turn left to Wolong Temple. Leaving the temple alley, turn left and south, then right to the Confucian Temple. Behind the temple is the Stele Forest. Turning left from the Confucian Temple and heading east leads to Dongzi Temple. Leaving the temple and climbing the city wall, one faces the South Mountain to the south and can see the entire city to the north. South: South is South Main Street, which runs through the middle of East and West Wood Markets. Near the South Gate, turn left to Shuyuanmen Street. Entering the attached elementary school of the First Normal School, one finds the Ancient China Pagoda. Entering the First Normal School further inside, one finds the Sidapzhongtian Pavilion. Leaving the school and returning to the western entrance of West Wood Market, head north and turn left onto Mafangmen Street to find the Public Education Center. Leaving the center and heading south, turn right to find the Provincial Library. To the right of the library is the South Courtyard Gate, the commercial center of the city. West: West is West Main Street. Heading west and turning north leads to the Drum Tower. Northwest of the tower is the Great Tang Islamic Temple. Returning to West Main Street and going west again, on the right is the Prefectural City God Temple. Going further west and turning right to the north leads to West Wutai. North is Wanshou Palace. At the corner of the city wall is Lama Guangren Temple. Returning to West Main Street, nearing the West Gate, turn right to find Jianguo Park. Inside the West Gate barbican is the Great Sweet Water Well, the source of drinking water for the entire city. North: North is North Main Street. To West Huamen, turn right to find the New City, i.e., the old Imperial City (now the Pacification Commissioner's Office), which contains a small Stele Forest. Returning to West Huamen and heading west is the Provincial Government. The former residence of Empress Dowager Cixi of the Qing Dynasty is in front of the rear building of the government. Next to it is the Liseng Tower. To the north of the Provincial Government's west side is Lianhu Park. (B) The Four Suburbs: East: Going east out of Zhongshan, one sees Hansenzhong Tomb to the south at Erdu. Going down Chang Le Po, one sees Baling Yuan to the south, which contains the tomb of Emperor Wen of the Han Dynasty. Further east across the Chan Bridge (ten li from the city) and the Ba Bridge (twenty li from the city) leads to Lintong City (fifty li from Xijing). South of the city at Linliu is Huaqing Pool at the foot of Mount Li. Nearby is the mausoleum of Emperor Qin Shi Huang. The women's school in the city has Wei stele inscriptions. South: Going south out of the South Gate leads to Jianfu Temple, which has the Tang Jianfu Temple Pagoda (commonly known as the Small Wild Goose Pagoda). Further south is Quanxingshan Temple. Southeast is Ci'en Temple, which has the Tang Great Wild Goose Pagoda. Northeast of Ci'en Temple is Leyouyuan, which has Qinglong Temple. Southeast is the ancient Qujiang Pool and Wudian Slope. Southwest of this area is Song Family Garden, Sanmenkou, and Mutasi Temple. Going south along the main road leads to Weiqu Town (twenty li from the city). To the west, one can see He General Mountain Forest, Qingliang Temple, Ducheng Dingkun Pool, etc. To the left of Weiqu Town is Huangzipo, above which is Shaoling Yuan. To the northeast on the Yuan, one can see the Du Mausoleum of Emperor Xuan of the Han Dynasty, and to the southeast, the Shaoling Mausoleum of Empress Xu. Leaving the town, the plain widens into Fanchuan, the food fief of Fan Kuai of the Han Dynasty. Going east, one passes Niutousi Temple, Du Gongbu Shrine, and Huayan Temple (the ancestral temple of the Huayan school has the Huayan Pagoda). To Duqu Town (thirty-five li from the city) is Xingjiao Temple, which has the three-shou pagodas of Xuanzang, Kuiji, and Yuanze (forty li from the city). Passing Yinjiahui, Kuyubridge, and Fengliangyuan leads to Tangyu (eighty li from the city). The hot springs of Tangyu are commonly known as Holy Water. To the east is Chuan (over a hundred li from the city). From Duqu Town, passing the Duqu riverbed, southwest to Sihaocun and Taiyi Palace. East of the palace, Baidaoyu has Jiawutai. Dayu has Lianhua Cave, Zheboyu has Yuhuang Temple and Dajing. Kuyu has Daxingshan, all famous places. Reaching Taiyi Palace leads to the foot of Cuihua Mountain (the mountain is over ten li high). On the mountain are Shuizhuchi, and to the west of the pool are Fengdong and Bingdong, Yang Si General Cave, etc. To the south are Jiaolong Cave Waterfall and Wuwuo Double Waterfall. To the east is Jinhualuo (above which is the Jinhua Miss Temple). West of Cuihua Mountain is South Wutai (over twenty li high). Behind South Wutai, the same mountain road connects with the foot of Cui Mountain. Going west seven or eight li from Taiyi Palace via Sihaocun leads to Liucun (sixty li from the city), which is the front foot of South Wutai. There are many temples on the mountain: San Sheng Temple, Bai Yi Tang, Da Ci Tang, Wu Fo Dian, Chaotianmen, Yitianmen, Guanyin Temple, Wan Bai Shu, Baosheng Spring, Xifang Jing, passing Xian Bridge, down Baoquan, Cihang An, Shang Baoquan, Yuanguang Tang, Er Tianmen, Gu Hun Tang, Puji Tai, Shengmu Dian, Yingzhen Gong, Lingguan Dian, Wu Sheng Dian, Liuli Dian, Shi Fo Dian, Qian Fo Si, San Tianmen, Lu Zu Xinggong, San Fo Si, San Sheng Gong, Hei Hu Dian, Nanhai Dian Zizhu Lin, Si Tianmen, etc., to the most famous Wutai, i.e., Da Tai, Wenshu Tai, Qingliang Tai, Lingyin Tai, She Shen Tai. From Liucun via Yusu Chuan, north over Mengxi Gong to Wangqu (over fifty li from the city), is the Tianxia Du Chenghuang Temple. Crossing the Mahetan Bridge and going west to Ziwu Town (sixty li from the city), to its south is Small Wutai. Further west to Fengyukou (seventy li from the city, fifteen li from Ziwu Town), inside the entrance to the mountain is Jingye Temple. Northwest to Lingqi Temple (over sixty li from the city, seven or eight li from Fengyukou). At the foot of the mountain between Liucun and Ziwu Town is the Pagoda Temple. In the mountain is Pei Gong Cave. From Linggan Temple, looking west at Zigge and Guifeng Mountains, in the mountain is the Baolin Pagoda, built by Yuchi Gong, with exquisite structure, unseen before. Below the mountain is Caotang Temple (fifteen li from Linggan Temple), the ancestral temple of Kumarajiva's Sanlun School, with the most famous Kumarajiva Jade Pagoda. Going northeast from Linggan Temple to Gaoqiao (fifty li from the city) leads to Xiangji Temple (forty li from the city), the ancestral temple of the Pure Land School, with a famous pagoda inside. Passing Shenhe Yuan and via Shenjia Bridge (about thirty li from the city, ten li from Xiangji Temple), go north back to the city. West: Going west out of the West Gate, passing the airport, crossing Feng Bridge and Xianyang Ferry (forty-five li from the city), northwest and up Zhou Mausoleum. Further north to Jinghui Canal and Luohui Canal (thirty or forty li from Zhou Mausoleum). Going west again down Yuan and entering Dianping, one finds Ma Pao Spring (about sixty li from the city). Up to Maoling, the tombs of Lady Li, Wei Qing, and Huo Qubing, Huo's tomb with stone carvings of horses trampling the Xiongnu, and the Maoling Public Education Area and a primary school. Further west down the mausoleum to Mawei, where the tomb of Yang Guifei is located (about seventy or eighty li from the city). Further west to Wugong County (over a hundred li from Xijing) are Jiang Yuan, Hou Ji, and Su Wu Temples and tombs. Looking north from Maoling is Zhaoling (about fifty li from Maoling). In central Shanbei County is the Yellow Emperor's Mausoleum (three or four hundred li from Zhou Mausoleum). From the West Gate, southwest to E County, along the way are Epang Palace, Kunming Pool, and King Wen Lingtai, etc. North: Going north out of the North Gate, turn right to the Railway Station, a newly built palace-style building, magnificent and splendid. North of the station is the Tang Daming Palace ruins, including Hanyuan Hall, Penglai Hall, Jinluan Hall, etc., where ancient sites can still be found. To its east is the East Inner Garden, to the west is the West Inner Garden, and to the north is the Forbidden Garden. The situation of Wangchun Pool in the east of the garden is still visible. Other sites such as Liyuan and Ningbi Pool still need to be verified.

18. Coal Mines and Porcelain Industry in Tongguan

Two hundred and forty li northwest of Shaanxi, along the Xianyu Highway directly to Tongguan County, the county has been known for its coal and porcelain industries. The mineral layers are abundant, and the coal quality is pure. Since the Longhai Railway directly reaches Xi'an, various emerging machine industries need coal. Therefore, it is an urgent task to develop national resources and open up the northwest frontier by designing scientific methods to mine coal. Tongguan porcelain, from the Song Dynasty to the present, is sold in Shanxi and Shaanxi provinces. The texture is hard and can reflect the Jingdezhen porcelain in the north and south. The people of the Northwest have always liked to buy and use it, but foreign goods are flooding in, making it easy to be squeezed out and gradually eliminated. If it is not improved, it will be difficult to expand sales, and the status of the porcelain industry will be completely robbed by imported goods. The following is a record of the mining of coal mines and the manufacturing of porcelain industry. (A) Coal Mine: Tongguan Coal Mine starts from Tongshugou in the west, and extends northeast along Longtou Mountain, passing through Chenlu Town in the middle, and ending at Chenjiahe, with a total length of 120 li. There are more than 30 coal kilns in the county. It is said that the coal mine there was unusually developed ten years ago. Since the 18th year of the Republic of China, it has suffered from natural disasters and man-made disasters, and most of the coal kilns have declared Hele. At present, there are only more than ten places such as Huiduipo, Xincun, and Chenjiahe. However, the coal seams in each place are very rich. The coal well is about 190 feet to 380 feet deep. There are one or two layers of coal seams, and the layer thickness is 5 feet to 3 zhang. For example, the coal in Huiduipo has two layers, each layer is 5 feet thick, the coal in Chenjiahe is 1 zhang and 2 feet thick, and the coal in Bailing is 3 zhang thick. The remaining coal seams are 7 or 8 feet thick on average. As for the East Kiln Town mud coal, it is 9 inches thick. Each kiln produces more than 3 tons of coal per day. According to the local price, each ton is worth 5 yuan. The organization of the coal nest has no large-scale coal factory. Except for those who operate independently, most of them jointly mine and sell separately. That is, a coal well is owned by several families. According to the number of shares, the labor cost of going to the bottom of the well is divided, and the coal produced by Quan Huan is distributed according to the number of inputs. The mining method is the oldest manual mining. Underground workers use iron tools to excavate. A huge pulley is placed at the wellhead, and eight people per class turn it up by manpower. Each resolution can take up to 200 catties of coal. Except for Huiduipo and Xincun, the coal reserves of the Siguan Coal Cellar are particularly rich. Cars and mule carts can drive directly into the interior, which is very convenient for mining and transportation. (B) Porcelain Industry: Tongguan porcelain, those who engage in the porcelain industry do not have sufficient capital, and are struggling with life. For all products, they only seek to ship goods quickly, and do not seek exquisite production. Most of the important works such as painting and glazing are entrusted to women and child laborers to perfunctorily deal with the matter. Daily production is calculated entirely by numbers, regardless of the quality of the beauty. As a result, the products are becoming more and more inferior. The original places of porcelain production were Huangbao, Lidi, Shangdian, Chenlu and other towns. Today, only Chenlu Town remains. The business is still good. Among them, the porcelain of Huangbao Town has the earliest history. It was founded in the Yongzhong period of the Jin Dynasty and stopped operating in the Xining period of the Song Dynasty. The porcelain products produced are also very wonderful, with delicate patterns. The existing porcelain can be sold at a high price for buying antiques, and it is regarded as a rare treasure. The organization of the kiln industry, there are four types of porcelain making in the Chenlu Town area: Bowl Kiln, specializing in burning bowls, dishes, etc.; Black Kiln, specializing in burning pots, urns, jars, cans, etc.; Urn Kiln, specializing in burning urns, large vats, large basins, etc.; Small Goods Kiln, specializing in burning bottles, pots, cups, inkstones, and miscellaneous small items, etc. Different categories are separated, and each does not interfere with the other. The soil used is all mined from the mountains in this area, and the coal burned is also produced locally. Unfortunately, the manufacturing still adheres to the old method of manual pottery firing. For example, when making bowls, the raw materials of the porcelain clay are placed on the stone, and another wooden stick is used to press and move the stone to rotate. Each push makes a bowl and takes it to be burned. This way of shipping goods is not only not fast, but also rough in production. It seems that it should be greatly improved. There are about 300 to 400 households in the kiln area, and there are 120 to 130 kiln caves, most of which are buildings from the Song Dynasty. There are less than 10 large kilns, about 30 medium-sized kilns, and 60 to 70 small kilns. Each kiln is built with an average of more than 10,000 bricks, and it can be burned twice a year, which is worth 1,500 to 600 yuan. According to statistics, the annual turnover is quite large, about more than 200,000.

Lu Provincial Government Takes Over Lufeng Yarn Factory Lufeng Stopped Work on February 9 After the Provincial Government Takes Over, It Will Continue to Operate 93

Jinan Communication, Lufeng Yarn Factory, is the largest and earliest yarn factory in Lu Province's private sector. In the past, its business was very prosperous for a while. However, in recent years, science and technology have advanced by leaps and bounds, and new machines have emerged one after another. Therefore, the existing machinery in the factory is outdated and old. Not only does it consume a lot, but the production is also small. In addition, the manager of the factory is not good at management. On February 9 this year, it was announced that the factory would be shut down. More than 2,000 workers suddenly lost their jobs. They have repeatedly sent representatives to the provincial authorities to request that the factory be ordered to start work quickly in order to maintain their livelihood. The authorities also believe that the factory has defaulted on a loan of 670,000 yuan from Minsheng Bank, which has not been repaid. It is a big problem to add so many unemployed people to the society. In order to maintain the livelihood of these unemployed workers and the continued existence of this great enterprise, Miao Xingcun, a provincial government consultant and chairman of the Jinan Grain Association and general manager of Chengtong Yarn Factory, was sent to take over the factory. Miao believed that the legal issues such as the share capital of the yarn factory and the debts of Minsheng Bank had not been resolved, so the takeover matters needed to be considered. Before the takeover, the three departments of the Department of Finance, the Department of Construction, and the Department of Finance decided that Minsheng Bank would invest money and Miao Xingcun would lease it on behalf of the bank, paying a certain amount of rent every month. The profits and losses would be borne by Chengtong Yarn Factory. On the morning of the 8th, Gong Xingcun immediately went to the factory with Police Commander Wu Huawen. In addition to counting the machinery accounts one by one, Gong Xingcun personally spoke to all the employees, and the factory would officially start work within days. As for how the factory will proceed in the future, it is said that Miao Xingcun intends to follow the spirit of running the Chengtong Yarn Factory, improving Lufeng, striving to increase production and reduce consumption, and using one year as the deadline for rectification, depending on the results, and then deciding everything (28th).

Jiaoji Railway Shortens Travel Time 94

——And Will Add Qingjing or Qinghu Through Train—— Jinan Communication, Jiaoji Railway cooperated with Jinpu Beineng Railways last year and implemented Qingping through train. After three months, it was suspended. It is now planned to resume it from April 1 to facilitate passengers on both sides. The Jiaoji Railway is recently planning to shorten the travel time between Jiqing sections 21 and 22, so that the train can arrive in Ji early to connect with the Jinpu Railway train. The Jiaoji Railway Bureau has scheduled a meeting on the 8th in Qingdao to convene the heads of each section of the entire railway's train machinery to study the problem of shortening the time. It is heard that it is planned to open Qingdao section 21 and Qinan section 21 every day at 1:30 pm. It takes 9 hours to travel to the destination at 10:30 pm (the current 12 fast train takes 9 and a half hours to arrive). No extra charge will be charged, and free tickets may also be applicable. Passengers can have a morning of leisure in Qingdao or Jinan to handle affairs and complete them before getting on the train again. They don't have to stay on the train for the month, which is extremely convenient for passengers. The method of shortening the travel time is because each passenger train must stop at each station to allow passengers to get on and off, or to load and unload goods. In the future, the 21st and 22nd trains will decide not to stop at small stations, and only stop at large stations such as Jinan Huang. Stop at larger stations such as Zaozhuang, Zhoucun Zhangdian, Xindian, Qingzhou, Changle or Weixian, Fangzi, Zuoshan, Gaomi, Jiaozhou, Chengyang, etc. to Cangkou, Sifang, Qingdao. At the same time, the bureau also pays attention to the passengers at each small station. Since the 21st and 22nd small stations do not stop, passengers at small stations will feel inconvenient. It is planned to add two additional trains to provide assistance, one from Qingdao to Weixian and one from Jinan to Fangzi, which will depart at 10:30 am every day. If this is done, passengers can be facilitated, but cargo may be slightly affected. Yang Chengxun, director of the Jinpu Railway Bureau, went to Qingdao the day before to discuss with Ge Guangting, chairman of the Jiaoji Railway Commission, and Shen Hong, mayor of Qingdao, and planned to add Qingdao-Nanjing or Qingdao-Shanghai through trains, imitating the Qingping through train method. One or two cars are hung on a certain train every day, and they are transferred to Jinan and hung on a certain train to the destination to facilitate passengers. In addition, the Jiaoji Railway had the worst business performance in the six months from June to the end of last year, losing more than 1 million yuan. After the New Year, the business turned better due to the active coal transportation, reaching a maximum of 58,000 yuan per day. Therefore, the current situation is still optimistic (27th).

Labor Service to Build the Ring Road

The 8th District Office of the county was ordered to handle the re-registration of reformed smokers, which was still considered diligent. A total of more than 180 smokers were registered. After the county government sent personnel to investigate and confirmed the facts, the opium-smoking clerk of the sub-office was dismissed and ordered to quit smoking. Registration of Prostitutes Completed Suzhou Divides Areas to Establish Public Prostitution, which has been registered since the beginning of registration until April, before it is completed. There are 18 first-class brothels with 39 prostitutes, located in Dongxi Minqingli and other places. There are 31 second-class brothels with 194 prostitutes, located in Tongchun, Tongle, Tongan and other neighborhoods, as well as Changchunfang Nantongle Dexianxiang Fu Taiyuanli. Business Tax Bureau Collects Taxes Directly

The business tax of various businesses in Suzhou has always been paid by the stores to the relevant industry associations, which are collected by the county chamber of commerce and transferred to the Business Tax Bureau. This method has been in place for several years. Recently, Feng Zhenya, the newly appointed director of the Business Tax Bureau, changed the collection method. From yesterday, he sent personnel to the streets to collect taxes from various stores. This collection is the spring tax of this year, but most of the stores have already paid it to the relevant industry associations and are preparing to collect it. Therefore, when the bureau staff sent personnel to collect taxes, they all reported it accordingly, but the bureau staff said that it must be collected directly. As a result, the stores reported to the relevant industry associations and reported to the chamber of commerce. The chamber of commerce was afraid that this would cause disputes. After discussing with the Standing Committee, it was decided to convene a general meeting of all members at 2 pm on March 3 to discuss countermeasures. The relevant industry associations and representatives of the store staff have been notified separately to attend the meeting.

A Cruel Mother-in-law Abuses Daughter-in-law, Leading to Murder

Robbery of a Large Sum of Money, Arrest on the Spot

Five bridge piers on the north bank are currently under construction separately. A large amount of materials such as steel beams and cement has been transported to the site. The pile-driving barges in the river center are operating swiftly and intensely as the machinery has been fully equipped. It is now understood that the entire bridge project, originally scheduled for completion at the end of this year, has been delayed by eight months and is now expected to be completed by the end of June next year.
